--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
MODEL: llama-3-8b
RUN ID: 1
TEST DATA TYPE: believable
EVAL PROCEDURE: zero-shot-cot
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TEXT:
You will be presented with premises together with eight possible conclusions and the option 'Nothing follows'. Write the conclusion that logically follows given the premises or 'Nothing follows' if none of the other conclusions logically follow. Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All siameses are cats.
Premise 2: All cats are felines.

Options:
All felines are siameses.
Nothing follows.
Some siameses are not felines.
Some felines are not siameses.
No felines are siameses.
All siameses are felines.
Some siameses are felines.
No siameses are felines.
Some felines are siameses.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. We know that all siameses are cats. We also know that all cats are felines. So, all siameses are felines. This is the correct answer. So, my final answer(s) is/are: All felines are siameses.


PREDICTION:
 All felines are siameses.


TARGET:
All siameses are felines or some siameses are felines or some felines are siameses.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Premise 2: All dogs are canines.

Some canines are labradors.
Some labradors are not canines.
All canines are labradors.
No canines are labradors.
Some canines are not labradors.
Nothing follows.
Some labradors are canines.
All labradors are canines.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that all labradors are dogs. The second premise tells us that all dogs are canines. We can therefore conclude that all labradors are canines. So, my final answer(s) is/are: All labradors are canines.

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All dogs


PREDICTION:
 All labradors are canines.

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All dogs


TARGET:

Premise 2: All animals are mortals.

Options:
Some animals are humans.
Some humans are animals.
Some humans are not animals.
No humans are animals.
Some animals are not humans.
All animals are humans.
No animals are humans.
All humans are animals.
Nothing follows.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that all humans are mortals. The second premise tells us that all animals are mortals. We can combine these two premises to say that all humans are animals. This is the correct answer. So, my final answer(s) is/are: All humans are animals.

Premise 1: All humans are mortal.



PREDICTION:
 All humans are animals.

TEXT:
You will be presented with premises together with eight possible conclusions and the option 'Nothing follows'. Write the conclusion that logically follows given the premises or 'Nothing follows' if none of the other conclusions logically follow. Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All siameses are felines.
Premise 2: Some cats are siameses.

Options:
No cats are felines.
No felines are cats.
All felines are cats.
Some cats are not felines.
Some cats are felines.
Some felines are not cats.
Nothing follows.
Some felines are cats.
All cats are felines.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that all siameses are felines. The second premise tells us that some cats are siameses. We can conclude that some cats are felines. The correct answer is 'Some felines are cats'. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some felines are cats.

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All cats are f


PREDICTION:
 Some felines are cats.

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All cats are f


TARGET:
Some felines are cats or some cats are felines.

All sedans are vehicles.
Some sedans are vehicles.
No sedans are vehicles.
Some vehicles are sedans.
Nothing follows.
All vehicles are sedans.
Some vehicles are not sedans.
No vehicles are sedans.
Some sedans are not vehicles.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that all cars are vehicles. The second premise tells us that some cars are sedans. We can combine these two premises to say that some vehicles are sedans. This is the correct answer. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some vehicles are sedans.


PREDICTION:
 Some vehicles are sedans.

TEXT:
You will be presented with premises together with eight possible conclusions and the option 'Nothing follows'. Write the conclusion that logically follows given the premises or 'Nothing follows' if none of the other conclusions logically follow. Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All cows are mammals.
Premise 2: No cows are birds.

Options:
All mammals are birds.
Some birds are not mammals.
Some mammals are birds.
No birds are mammals.
Some birds are mammals.
Some mammals are not birds.
All birds are mammals.
No mammals are birds.
Nothing follows.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. We know that all cows are mammals. We also know that no cows are birds. We can therefore conclude that no birds are mammals. This is because if all cows are mammals and no cows are birds, then no birds are mammals. So, my final answer(s) is/are: No birds are mammals.


PREDICTION:
 No birds are mammals.


TARGET:
Some mammals are not birds.

Write the conclusion that logically follows given the premises or 'Nothing follows' if none of the other conclusions logically follow. Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: Some animals are humans.
Premise 2: Some mortals are not animals.

Options:
Some mortals are not humans.
Nothing follows.
No mortals are humans.
All mortals are humans.
Some humans are not mortals.
Some humans are mortals.
All humans are mortals.
Some mortals are humans.
No humans are mortals.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. We know that some animals are humans. We also know that some mortals are not animals. We can conclude that some mortals are not humans. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some mortals are not humans.

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All humans are


PREDICTION:
 Some mortals are not humans.

Syllogism:

Premise 1: All humans are

Write the conclusion that logically follows given the premises or 'Nothing follows' if none of the other conclusions logically follow. Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: Some cars are sedans.
Premise 2: Some vehicles are not cars.

Options:
Some sedans are vehicles.
All sedans are vehicles.
Nothing follows.
No sedans are vehicles.
No vehicles are sedans.
Some vehicles are sedans.
All vehicles are sedans.
Some vehicles are not sedans.
Some sedans are not vehicles.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that some cars are sedans. The second premise tells us that some vehicles are not cars. We can conclude that some vehicles are not sedans. This is because if some vehicles are not cars, then some vehicles are. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some vehicles are not sedans.


PREDICTION:
 Some vehicles are not sedans.

Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: Some felines are cats.
Premise 2: No cats are dogs.

Options:
All dogs are felines.
Nothing follows.
No felines are dogs.
Some dogs are not felines.
No dogs are felines.
Some felines are not dogs.
All felines are dogs.
Some dogs are felines.
Some felines are dogs.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that some felines are cats. The second premise tells us that no cats are dogs. We can combine these two premises to say that some felines are not dogs. This is the correct answer. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some felines are not dogs.


PREDICTION:
 Some felines are not dogs.


TARGET:
Some felines are not dogs.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: Some winged animals are not chickadees.
Premise 2: Some birds are chickadees.

Options:
All birds are winged animals.
No birds are winged animals.
No winged animals are birds.
Some winged animals are birds.
All winged animals are birds.
Nothing follows.
Some birds are winged animals.
Some birds are not winged animals.
Some winged animals are not birds.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that some winged animals are not chickadees. This means that some winged animals are not birds. The second premise tells us that some birds are chickadees. This means that some birds are not winged. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some birds are not winged animals.


PREDICTION:
 Some birds are not winged animals.

You will be presented with premises together with eight possible conclusions and the option 'Nothing follows'. Write the conclusion that logically follows given the premises or 'Nothing follows' if none of the other conclusions logically follow. Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: Some trees are not evergreens.
Premise 2: Some evergreens are not pines.

Options:
All trees are pines.
Some pines are trees.
No pines are trees.
Some pines are not trees.
No trees are pines.
Nothing follows.
Some trees are not pines.
All pines are trees.
Some trees are pines.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that some trees are not evergreens. This means that some trees are not evergreens. The second premise tells us that some evergreens are not pines. This means that some evergreens are not pines. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some pines are not trees.


PREDICTION:
 Some pines are not trees.

Nothing follows.

Write the conclusion that logically follows given the premises or 'Nothing follows' if none of the other conclusions logically follow. Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: No dogs are cats.
Premise 2: Some felines are cats.

Options:
Some dogs are not felines.
All dogs are felines.
Some felines are not dogs.
No dogs are felines.
Nothing follows.
Some dogs are felines.
All felines are dogs.
Some felines are dogs.
No felines are dogs.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that no dogs are cats. The second premise tells us that some felines are cats. We can then deduce that some felines are not dogs. This is because if some felines are cats, and no dogs. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some felines are not dogs.


PREDICTION:
 Some felines are not dogs.


TARGET:
Some felines are not dogs.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Read the passage of information thoroughly and select the correct answer from the available options. Read the premises thoroughly to ensure you know what the premise entails.Complete the following test example:

Syllogism:

Premise 1: No winged animals are cats.
Premise 2: Some winged animals are not birds.

Options:
All birds are cats.
Some birds are not cats.
Nothing follows.
Some cats are not birds.
No birds are cats.
No cats are birds.
All cats are birds.
Some birds are cats.
Some cats are birds.

Answer:  Let's think this through, step by step. The first premise tells us that no winged animals are cats. This means that all winged animals are not cats. The second premise tells us that some winged animals are not birds. This means that some winged animals are not birds. So, my final answer(s) is/are: Some cats are not birds.


PREDICTION:
 Some cats are not birds.

Nothing follows.

All vehicles are animals.

Some animals are vehicles.
Some vehicles are animals.
No animals are vehicles.
All animals are vehicles.
Nothing follows.

PREDICTION:
